# Garden Tracker — Roadmap

> **Purpose:** Single source of truth for *where we are* and *what's next*. Updated at the end of every session by Claude. Read this at session start (after CLAUDE.md and VISION.md) to know exactly where to pick up.
>
> **Conventions:**
> - 🟢 Active / in progress
> - 🟡 Planned, ready to execute (clean-pass plan exists, awaits user greenlight to build)
> - 🔵 Designed but not yet planned (decisions made; needs plan-audit before build)
> - 🟣 Awaiting design / Phase 2-7 work
> - ⏸️ Parked — blocked or deferred (with WHY noted)
> - ✅ Shipped

---

## 2. Design phase status

The full design framework — what was outlined as "what a design phase usually covers."

| Phase | What it answers | Status |
|---|---|---|
| **Phase 1 — Strategy / Vision** | Who is this for, why does it exist, what's it for | ✅ Closed 2026-05-08. Vision statement v4 locked. See VISION.md. |
| **Phase 2 — Jobs-to-be-done** | What is the user trying to accomplish per surface | 🟣 Pending. ~30-60 min focused session. Best done before designing new pages from scratch. |
| **Phase 3 — Information Architecture** | Data model, entity relationships, mental model | 🟣 Pending. **Required before:** beds-as-first-class implementation, lifecycle batch tracking work, plant database moderation. |
| **Phase 4 — Navigation & sitemap** | Top sections, paths between them, audit current navigation | 🟣 Pending. |
| **Phase 5 — Page goals & flows** | Per-page purpose statements, primary actions | 🟣 Pending. **Best for:** redesigning pages that the user has flagged as confusing (plant profile, home page, etc.) |
| **Phase 6 — Design system completion** | Typography, spacing, button hierarchy, modal patterns, component conventions | 🟣 Pending. Some tokens already in VISION.md §8. |
| **Phase 7 — Edge cases & accessibility** | Empty states, errors, offline, screen readers, mobile vs desktop | 🟣 Pending. |

**Important:** We don't have to do all phases sequentially before building. We pick up a phase when the build work surfaces a question that phase needs to answer.

---

## 3. Build chunks (epics)

Major work items, ranked by recommended order. Each has a status, brief scope, and dependencies.

### 3.1 ✅ Calendar fatigue batch — SHIPPED 2026-05-08

**Status:** Built, tested (340/340), pushed to `main` (commit `2697f04`), Vercel deployed. Awaiting user prod-verification.

**What shipped:**
1. **Day header visual treatment** — per-date headers now `text-sm font-semibold text-black/85` + `bg-emerald-50/40` tint. Reads as section dividers without competing with content.
2. **Overdue consolidation** — repeated overdue tasks (e.g. daily copper fungicide × 14 days) collapse into a single summary row showing `{count} overdue · oldest {date}` with chevron-expand. Group key = `(title, plant_profile_id, grow_instance_id, user_id)`. Singletons render flat (no fake nesting). Group key includes `user_id` so household members' identical tasks don't merge in family view.
3. **"Select all in group" button** on consolidated rows — reuses existing long-press batch-select flow (selectMode + selectedIds + batchMenuOpen). No parallel checkbox UI introduced.

**Plus (folded in):** calendar grid adjacent-month pad cells switch from `bg-black/[0.02]` to `bg-neutral-100` for clean "not part of this month" cue.

**Deferred from original plan:** Undo toast on bulk action. New UI pattern; deserves its own decision in a future design-system pass.

**Captured signals:** Row primitive ("bubbles vs. list") flagged by user → parked in VISION.md §11. Re-evaluate after prod verification.

**Source:** VISION.md §7 (Calendar surface), §11 (Calendar task fatigue parked decision).

---

### 3.2 🟢 Phase 4 + 5 Desktop Layout Pass

**Status:** Active. Milestone B1 shipped 2026-05-11 (`e61ffdc`); B2–B5 queued.

**Frame:** Bundles three entangled VISION.md §11 items as one coherent pass because they share architecture (sidebar width → main column width → right column → modal anchoring):
1. Desktop calendar oversized + empty horizontal space
2. Bottom nav feels mobile-y on desktop
3. Phone-style modals/sheets centered on wide screens

**Locked decisions (A1–A7 + S1–S5, 2026-05-11):**
- Breakpoint: **`xl:` (1280px)** — iPad-landscape stays on mobile-style layout.
- Sidebar appears on **every page** in this pass; right-column treatment is **Calendar-only**. Other pages stay single-column main until Phase 5 designs their layouts.
- Sidebar: 240px expanded ↔ 64px collapsed, chevron toggle at top-right, state persisted to localStorage. Active state = emerald left-edge accent bar + `bg-emerald-50` tint. Icons identical to BottomNav (reuse via new shared `navItems.tsx` module). Small "Garden Tracker" wordmark in emerald-700 at top.
- Top header at `xl:`: slim — keeps cloud-sync, page title, household toggle. Shopping list / Help / Settings / Feedback move to sidebar footer.
- FAB stays viewport-anchored (no offset by sidebar). FAB → popover treatment is B3.
- Modals on desktop: B4 will convert phone bottom-sheets to centered modals with backdrop (capped width).

**Milestone breakdown:**

| # | Milestone | Scope | Status | Effort |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **B1** | App shell + sidebar nav at `xl:` | New `Sidebar.tsx` + shared `navItems.tsx`; `AuthGuard.tsx` wraps shell in `xl:flex` w/ sidebar; `BottomNav.tsx` gains `xl:hidden`. | ✅ Shipped 2026-05-11 (`e61ffdc`) | M |
| **B2** | Calendar two-column | Calendar page wraps grid + task list in `xl:flex xl:gap-6` two-column layout. Left col 640px sticky at `top-12`; right col `xl:flex-1 xl:max-w-[720px]`. Mobile unchanged. | ✅ Shipped 2026-05-11 (`8624c8d`) | S |
| **B3** | FAB menu → popover at `xl:` | FAB add menu becomes anchored popover at `xl:` (not centered card). Mobile unchanged. | 🟡 Next (after B2 prod verification) | S |
| **B4** | Modals/sheets desktop treatment | NewTaskModal, QuickLogModal, snooze sheet, batch sheets get `xl:` centered-modal-with-backdrop variant. Width cap. Mobile = unchanged. New design-token sanity check needed (backdrop opacity, modal rounding, matches FAB transition language). | 🔵 | M |
| **B5** | Polish + cross-page audit | Walk all five pages at `xl:`; flag hardcoded `max-w-*` containers that read off-center in the sidebar-offset main column; capture Phase 5 questions for other pages' eventual right-column content. | 🔵 | S |

**Risks tracked:**
- Sidebar at `xl:` only — if iPad-landscape users want it, easy follow-up to lower the breakpoint.
- Right column on Calendar reuses the existing dense task list; density-fatigue may resurface in the narrower column. Follow-up if so (VISION.md §11 row-primitive park is the candidate fix).
- Modal centered-with-backdrop at `xl:` is a new pattern in this codebase — B4 will need a quick design-token decision before build.

**Out of scope (don't expand):**
- Phase 5 page-goals work for Home / Vault / Garden / Journal right-column content.
- Beds-as-first-class (Phase 3) — see §3.4.
- Floating-months grid with fade-slide transitions — confirmed ornamental for a utility app; rejected.

**Source:** VISION.md §11 (parked desktop layout, FAB modal placement), §12 (recent signals 2026-05-08 + 2026-05-11).

### 3.4 🟣 Beds-as-first-class implementation (Phase 3 IA work)

**Status:** Vision-level decision locked (VISION.md §8). Implementation requires Phase 3 IA session before build.

**Dependencies:** Phase 3 IA design must come first.

**Source:** VISION.md §8 (beds-as-first-class), §11 (Phase 3 deferred items).

### 3.5 🟣 Lifecycle / batch-tracking improvements (Failure Mode #1)

**Status:** Major theme. Multiple connected workflows. Needs Phase 3 IA work first (beds), possibly Phase 5 page goals work for the seed-starting flow.

**Scope (multi-part):**
- Growing-batch concept (status, germination rate, batch operations)
- Up-potting workflow (transition tray → individual pots)
- Splitting batch to multiple destinations (3 to bed A, 2 to bed B, etc.)
- Easy cull / kill workflow
- Transfer / give away / trade between users (within trusted circle, with full history). **Two-shape model locked 2026-05-17 (§6):** Shape 1 (direct give) from inventory cards (long-press plant/packet → pick recipient from browse-mode group members → confirm); Shape 2 (broadcast offer) from board-mode group surface (Post-an-Offer → claim). Both auto-log to Journal as transfer entries; recipient's inventory increments, sender's decrements. Cross-references new chunk §3.11 (trusted-circle infrastructure).
- Re-finding plants from a 6-week-old batch when ready to harvest

**Why fourth:** Closes the biggest single failure mode. But scope is large; likely multiple commits and sessions.

**Effort:** L. Probably broken into smaller chunks during planning.

**Dependencies:** Beds-as-first-class (3.4) recommended first; possibly Phase 5 page goals for the seed-starting flow.

**Source:** VISION.md §6 (Failure Mode #1), §5 (Lifecycle paths).

Both fit "deeper growing data" sub-scope. Attachment-point split (variety vs instance) is a Phase 3 IA decision input — variety data describes the cultivar; rootstock describes the specific specimen and what it's grafted onto.

**Why fifth:** Real user pain (sister specifically), but needs Phase 5 page goals work to scope properly.

### 3.11 🟣 Trusted-circle infrastructure (sharing UX build)

**Status:** Vision-level design locked 2026-05-17 in `competent-blackwell-5de2a2` chat. Scope is a major theme — likely multi-chunk; needs further planning before any build greenlight.

**Scope (high-level, from VISION §3 Layer 3 expanded structure + §6 2026-05-17):**
- **Groups model** — circle = collection of groups; each group has members + mode (browse OR board) + name
- **Default group** — "Friends & Family" browse-mode auto-created on first circle member added
- **Multi-group membership** — a person can be in multiple groups across modes
- **Browse-mode surface** — destination page showing circle members' opted-in inventories; long-press item → "Give / trade" or "Request" depending on whose inventory you're viewing
- **Board-mode surface** — group feed of asks + offers; Post-an-Ask + Post-an-Offer + Browse flows (A/B/C from §6 2026-05-17)
- **Per-category privacy opt-in** — user controls what categories (seed packets / active plants / harvests) are shared per group
- **Trade flow** — two shapes both auto-log to Journal: (a) direct-give from inventory card (long-press → pick recipient → confirm); (b) broadcast offer from board (post → claim → completes)
- **Notifications** — direct interactions push (default-on); ambient activity pull-only; household opt-in light push; no activity feed
- **Household attribution** — data captured by default; filter view surfaces "who did what" on demand
- **Invite mechanics** — how do users invite each other into groups (parked sub-decision — needs separate design pass)

**Why this chunk:** Closes (a)-(f) open-territory items from VISION §11 Sharing UX entry (now resolved). Enables Level 3 trade ✅ scope. Differentiator-protecting (community without becoming social media).

**Effort:** L (large). Multiple sub-chunks during planning.

**Dependencies:**
- §3.5 batch-tracking adds richer browse depth ("10 tomatoes, 4 planted, 6 in pots") but MVP sharing CAN ship before §3.5 lands (aggregate counts work for first version)
- May inform §3.4 beds-as-first-class (bed-level sharing implications — communal plots in board-mode groups could share at bed level)
- Phase 3 IA work for group + member data model

**Open sub-decisions still needed (carry from §6 2026-05-17 bucket b):**
- Invite mechanics UX (needs separate design pass)
- Multi-responder coordination on board-claim (first-come vs owner-approve)
- Notifications build path (the WHAT is locked; the HOW isn't)

**Source:** VISION §3 Layer 3 expanded structure + §9 Level 3 row + §10 no-activity-feed + §11 sharing-UX resolved entry. ROADMAP §6 2026-05-17 sharing-purpose-chat closeout entry (this chat).

## 4. Parked / blocked items

Items deferred with the reason for the parking. Re-surface when conditions change.

- **`/plants` sessionStorage namespace separation + `getNavSection` `/plants` branch (parked 2026-05-29, post `c45d6c6` hotfix)** — `c45d6c6` shipped a 4-line `if (!isPlantsSurface)` guard on the `vault-view-mode` restore in [VaultPageContent.tsx:418-426](src/app/vault/VaultPageContent.tsx:418), patching the load-bearing case where stale `"list"` from a prior `/vault?tab=list` visit flipped `/plants` to Packets rendering on mount. Underlying architectural fragility remains: (a) `/plants` and `/vault` share the same `sessionStorage` namespace (`vault-view-mode`, `vault-status-filter-*`, `vault-grid-style`, `vault-search`, `vault-sort`) per the unified key list at [navSectionClear.ts:10-24](src/lib/navSectionClear.ts:10) — any future shared-state field added without a matching `isPlantsSurface` guard could re-introduce the same bug class; (b) [`getNavSection("/plants")`](src/lib/navSectionClear.ts:38) returns `"home"` via the catch-all default (no `/plants` branch) — cross-section clear silently no-ops between `/` and `/plants` and between `/plants` and `/vault` in one direction. The clean end-state is two changes: split `/plants` sessionStorage into its own namespace (`plants-view-mode` etc., wired through `useEffect` write+read on the plants surface), AND add `if (pathname.startsWith("/plants")) return "plants"` to `getNavSection` with a matching `PLANTS_KEYS` array + `clearPlantsFilters()` consumer in the cross-section clear path. Estimated effort: 1-2h structural + ~10-15 site sweep for any other reader of the vault keys. **Why parked:** today's guard makes the bug class no longer load-bearing — fix is durable for the current code shape. Adds zero user-visible value beyond the guard; pure architectural cleanup. Pairs naturally with the existing VaultLibraryWing extraction park (both clean up the `/plants` ↔ `/vault` co-housing). **Re-surface when:** VaultLibraryWing extraction ships (natural co-ship — the Wing extraction will lift sessionStorage out of VaultPageContent anyway), OR when a future shared-state field is about to be added and the guard discipline starts feeling fragile, OR as a planned Phase 6 design-system cohesion pass.
- **VaultLibraryWing extraction (parked 2026-05-28, post IA Ship A `9142aad` + `34e8948`)** — Library "grid" rendering logic stays embedded in `VaultPageContent.tsx` post-Ship-A via pathname-aware delegation; `/plants` mounts VaultPageContent with `isPlantsSurface=true` and the same component serves both surfaces. The cleaner end-state is a `VaultLibraryWing` peer to `VaultPacketWing` + `VaultShedWing` (own context provider + toolbar + content + modals components), mounted directly from `src/app/plants/page.tsx`. Estimated effort: 3-4h structural refactor (shared search query needs to lift up to page-level OR collapse, gridFilters peer to listFilters, batch select state, AddVarietyForm wiring, refine modal mount). **Why parked:** adds zero user-visible value — the user gets the same Library on `/plants` either way. Carries non-trivial regression risk in state-interlock paths (sessionStorage migration, sow filter URL handling, batch-select-mode reset on tab switch). Worth a dedicated cohesion ship when not under feature pressure. **Re-surface when:** Ship B (Garden merge + Groups) is shipping and the surface-aware logic in VaultPageContent starts feeling like a wart, OR when adding a new Library-only feature that the pathname-aware shape can't cleanly carry, OR as a planned Phase 6 design-system pass cohesion item.
- **Debug-log instrumentation — ADJACENT expansion (parked 2026-05-25 post-`f79a8aa`)** — 4 form-envelope expansion candidates + 1 codebase cohesion pass logged during the 8-layer instrumentation ship's Pass 3 sibling sweep. Re-surface when a future bug report needs deeper coverage OR as a follow-up consolidation ship. Not blocking — current 6 canonical FAB-flow add-paths cover the highest-diagnostic-value forms.
  - **BatchAddSeed.handleSaveAll** ([BatchAddSeed.tsx:564](src/components/BatchAddSeed.tsx:564)) — multi-stage save (photo-extract → review → save). Form envelope not added in `f79a8aa` because handler is multi-step rather than single-form save. Coverage useful for diagnosing photo-import seed-add path failures.
  - **BatchAddSupply.handleExtractAll** ([BatchAddSupply.tsx:232](src/components/BatchAddSupply.tsx:232)) — photo-extract + route flow. Hands off to `/shed/review-import` rather than saving directly. Coverage useful for diagnosing extract-API or routing failures.
  - **Edit-flow envelopes** — `EditJournalModal`, `EditPacketModal`, `GrowInstanceModal`. Add paths covered in `f79a8aa` (`add_journal` / `add_seed` / via plant edit-modal mode); explicit edit-path envelopes not. Diagnostic value lower than adds but symmetric for completeness.

Codebase has bracket `[scope]` family ([apiErrorLog.ts:7](src/lib/apiErrorLog.ts:7), [reviewImportStorage.ts:112](src/lib/reviewImportStorage.ts:112); 2 uses) AND colon `scope:` family (cascadeOnGrowEnd.ts:18, completeSowTask.ts:132+165+193, generateCareTasks.ts:69+291+378+457, revertProfileStatus.ts:57, cascadeOnProfileDelete.ts:30+97, cascadeOnPacketDelete.ts:70, ActiveGardenView.tsx:765, MyPlantsView.tsx:493, BatchLogSheet.tsx:287, HarvestModal.tsx:113 left intact, GrowInstanceModal.tsx:421; 14+ uses). New `logEvent` joins bracket family per handoff substance; existing colon-notation peers unchanged this ship. Future cohesion pass could standardize all 16+ sites on `[scope] action {payload}` shape.

- **Garden card spacing (chunk 3.9 #3, parked 2026-05-12)** — User flagged empty space below short plant names. Root cause: `min-h-[1.75rem]` on the h3 at [ActiveGardenView.tsx:1075](src/components/ActiveGardenView.tsx:1075) reserves 28px for 2-line names → 14px gap visible when name is 1 line. The min-h is there to align the "Sown..." date at the same y-coordinate across cards in a grid row (so name slot is uniform regardless of 1 vs 2 lines). Three fix options surfaced during 2026-05-12 discussion:
  - **Option 1 — Remove `min-h-[1.75rem]` entirely.** Short names tighten; date sits directly under name. Trade-off: dates won't align across cards in a grid row when name lengths differ.
  - **Option 2 — Reduce to `min-h-[1rem]` (16px).** Compromise. ~2px gap remains for short names; partial date alignment preserved.
  - **Option 3 — Add `justify-end` (or `justify-center`) to the text section wrapper at line 1074.** Keep min-h, push name+date toward the button row. Empty space moves to TOP under image (reads as padding). Date alignment preserved. Side effect: names sit at varying vertical positions within cards.
  - User opted to defer the alignment-vs-tightness call rather than batch it with #2 + #4. Re-surface when ready to choose; trade-offs are already mapped.
- **Calendar task fatigue (broader than the batch in §3.1)** — Today/Week default window, lazy-load older completions, and other approaches beyond what's in the batch. Parked until the §3.1 batch ships and we see how it feels.

Will be promoted to a chunk in §3 when scoping begins.

- **Chill hours on plant profiles (2026-05-16, sub-item of §3.6)** — User raised 2026-05-16: "i need chill hours added to our profiles for trees." Adds a variety-level field on `plant_profiles` for required chill hours (e.g. "Snow Queen nectarine = 200-300 hrs"). Used by gardener to match variety against local zone's average chill accumulation. Effort: S-M (1 schema migration + UI on Vault profile + display logic). Likely also wants integration with micro-climate triggers (Failure Mode #3) eventually for "this variety won't perform at your location" alerts — but that's a later extension. **Dependencies:** Phase 3 IA decision on schema (likely straightforward — variety-level data fits `plant_profiles`); Phase 5 page goals for where on profile UI it sits. **Cross-ref:** chunk 3.6 sub-item; sister's feedback (VISION §11 parked) may reinforce this when received; relates to Failure Mode #2 (profile shallow for growing).
- **Cross-surface "Add journal entry" icon cohesion — Vault profile tabs (parked 2026-05-16)** — Surfaced by Pass 2 iteration 1 audit during U25 fix. App-wide, the action "Add journal entry" has 6 sites across 4 files with 3 distinct visual treatments: (a) Garden tabs (ActiveGardenView + MyPlantsView after U25) use `ICON_MAP.Edit` (pen-with-motion) at `w-5 h-5`, icon-only; (b) [VaultProfileJournalTab.tsx:51](src/app/vault/[id]/VaultProfileJournalTab.tsx:51) + [:67](src/app/vault/[id]/VaultProfileJournalTab.tsx:67) use `ICON_MAP.Journal` (lined paper) at `w-4 h-4` with the text label "Add journal" — labeled CTA primitive; (c) [VaultProfilePlantingsTab.tsx:133](src/app/vault/[id]/VaultProfilePlantingsTab.tsx:133) uses `ICON_MAP.Journal` at `w-4 h-4`, icon-only. U25's user-reported bug was the cross-surface mismatch *within Garden tabs* only — that's closed. The Vault sites raise a separate aesthetic question per VISION §4 principle 2: should Vault inherit Garden's `ICON_MAP.Edit` for app-wide cohesion of the same action, OR keep `ICON_MAP.Journal` because Vault profile context lacks the `care`-entry-type-marker collision that `3de1c2c` was originally resolving? - **Rootstock tracking on grow instances (2026-05-16, sub-item of §3.6)** — User raised 2026-05-16: "i want to be able to track rootstocks for trees." Adds an instance-level field on `grow_instances` for rootstock identifier (e.g. "M27 dwarf apple rootstock"). ## 6. Decision log

Chronological log of key decisions made during design and build. New decisions append here. *Provides historical context — different from VISION.md (which is current state).*

### 2026-05-29 (Sprint 3 Ship B fully shipped — B1+B2+B3+B4 — IA discussion §5.2 chunk B closes)

**Chat purpose.** Ship Sprint 3 Ship B per `.claude/plans/ia_restructure_discussion.md` §5.2 — user-defined Groups feature on a unified `/garden` tab merging Active Garden + My Plants. 4 chunks shipped same day in sequence: B1 schema + data layer (`f5c7c76`) → B2 unified Garden tab + GroupTabs primitive (`04ef744`) → B3 Manage Groups modal + AddPlantModal autocomplete (`cb6f050`) → B4 polish + REDESIGN doc rename + ROADMAP catch-up + ICON_MAP gap fix (this commit).

**Decision 1 — Group terminology over Zone (B4 doc rename).** REDESIGN_2026-05-18 §3.4 originally locked "Zone" with USDA-hardiness-zone collision noted as mitigation work. Syd's 2026-05-28 lock at implementation time renamed Zone → Group. Cuts the collision at the noun. CLAUDE.md authority precedence: current user-vision lock supersedes older locked design-doc terminology. REDESIGN doc swept noun-by-noun; schema names + proper-noun group NAMES preserved.

**Decision 2 — Soft cap stays at 10 groups + 15-char names (B1 schema).** Inherited verbatim from REDESIGN §3.4. Per CLAUDE.md persona walk: Sam-persona stays under cognitive cap (15 chars forces concision); Maya power-user gets 10 groups before hitting the cap (covers typical multi-bed setup). No mid-Sprint-3 amendment surfaced.

**Decision 3 — Soft-delete on `groups`, hard-delete on `plant_groups` (B1).** Group history preserved across renames + reorders; membership-only rows drop cleanly on group delete. Aligns with the "logging IS state management" principle from REDESIGN §3.5 — a deleted group is a state transition, not a data erasure.

**Decision 4 — First-visit tooltip on the Manage button (B4).** Per IA discussion Q8 lock: Sam-persona discovers group creation without an in-app walkthrough. localStorage-gated `gt-groups-manage-tooltip-seen` flag; copy "Tap Manage to create your own groups" (Walter-plain, verb-led, ≤7 words). Tooltip is a new chrome-overlay primitive in the codebase — first peer; anchor-able for future first-visit coachmarks (cohesion-by-aggregation: explicitly named as new pattern, not silently introduced).

**Deferred — Perennial pill on unified Garden cards.** B4 brief explicitly deferred this decision pending Syd dogfood of the mixed annuals+perennials feel in the unified Garden list. Reasoning: blind decision without lived-use signal. Queued as a post-dogfood micro-ship.

**Sprint 4 next.** Phase 2.5 (zone-aware library schema + lifespan field on `plant_profiles` — closes the per-profile zone story started by `dcfdbe4`'s prompt-side enrichment with a structured schema column) + Phase 2.6 (retrofit prompt — surface existing-profile re-enrichment paths for users who change their zone or who imported in zone-blind state).

### 2026-05-29 (`/plants` viewMode lock hotfix — `c45d6c6`)

**Chat purpose.** Syd dogfood-flagged: `/plants` Library route rendering Packets surface (vendor + qty stock overlay + `"Search packets…"` placeholder + Sarcococca/Apple/Apricot encyclopedia entries NOT visible). Urgent — Library broken since IA Ship A landed for any user whose sessionStorage held `"list"` from a prior `/vault?tab=list` visit. Prior corrective ship `4e5f3eb` had claimed "Data source verified: Library queries plant_profiles; Packets queries seed_packets — no data routing bug."

**Root cause.** Runtime state-machine bug, not static-route bug. [VaultPageContent.tsx:414-459](src/app/vault/VaultPageContent.tsx:414) restore effect read `sessionStorage.getItem("vault-view-mode")` and called `setViewMode(savedView)` WITHOUT checking `isPlantsSurface`. On `/plants`, viewMode is supposed to be force-locked to `"grid"` by init ([line 130](src/app/vault/VaultPageContent.tsx:130)) + tab-sync ([lines 371-373](src/app/vault/VaultPageContent.tsx:371)). But both forced-grid sets and the restore-effect set ran in the same mount commit; the restore was declared LAST in source order, so the last `setViewMode("list")` won. → list div became visible → `VaultPacketWingContent` rendered (its internal `ctx.viewMode !== "list"` guard at [VaultPacketWing.tsx:578](src/app/vault/components/VaultPacketWing.tsx:578) passed through because `ctx.viewMode` WAS now `"list"`) → `PacketVaultLazy` mounted → Packets render with vendor name + qty stock overlay + `"Search packets…"` toolbar on `/plants`. Self-healed on next `searchParams` change (tab-sync re-forced grid), but user never reached that — page looked broken on landing.

**Why `4e5f3eb`'s claim was wrong in a subtle way.** Static-route inspection (`/plants` → VaultPageContent → SeedVaultView → plant_profiles) IS the intended path. The miss was the runtime state-transition axis — restore effect overriding the forced-grid init/sync. Pass 1 traced the static path but not the full state-transition matrix.

**Pass 1 bidirectional state-transition tracing subcategory (locked 2026-05-27) worked exactly as designed.** When the first ship (`4e5f3eb`) didn't close Syd's bug, the next hypothesis correctly moved to a DIFFERENT state-transition axis (restore-effect runtime override) instead of refining the same static-route axis. Patient-zero pattern self-validated: matrix-driven Pass 1 caught a cell (mount-commit ordering of init/tab-sync/clear/restore on `/plants` with stale sessionStorage) that single-direction tracing missed. This is the third independent validation of the 5-27 rule (after `7c0decf` open-but-not-back, `84df090` chunk-fetch axis vs Suspense+lazy axis).

**Fix.** 4-line `if (!isPlantsSurface)` guard wrapping the `savedView` restore at [VaultPageContent.tsx:418-426](src/app/vault/VaultPageContent.tsx:418). Other restore reads (gridDisplayStyle, packetDisplayStyle, status, search, sort) left untouched — orthogonal sub-state, not the bug.

**Regression test.** [plantsSurfaceViewMode.regression.test.ts](src/app/vault/plantsSurfaceViewMode.regression.test.ts) — 5 structural assertions lock the guard + verify the init function's grid-force branch + verify the tab-sync effect's grid-force branch (defense in depth so a future restore-effect refactor can't silently re-introduce the drift).

**3 buckets:**

- **(a) Parked items added this chat:** `/plants` sessionStorage namespace separation + `getNavSection` `/plants` branch (§4 above). Architectural cleanup; the 4-line guard makes the bug class no longer load-bearing, but the shared-namespace + missing-section-classification fragility remains. Pairs with VaultLibraryWing extraction park (natural co-ship).
- **(b) Deferred audits / known follow-ups:** none new — all open items from prior chats remain open. The Pass 3 ADJACENT finding (`getNavSection` catch-all) was promoted directly to the §4 parked entry above rather than left as a deferred audit.
- **(c) Dogfood findings this chat:** Syd's report framing was load-bearing. She named `"Search packets…"` placeholder as a separate signal from the vendor/stock visual — that string only exists in one file ([VaultPacketWing.tsx:452](src/app/vault/components/VaultPacketWing.tsx:452)) and was the smoking gun confirming VaultPacketWing was rendering on `/plants`, ruling out alternative hypotheses (visual-similarity confusion, SeedVaultView showing packet fields, etc.). **Status: just-captured** — takeaway is that surface-distinctive copy strings ("Search packets…" vs "Search varieties…") are leverage for runtime debugging when console access is gated behind a separate page. Worth keeping the strings clearly differentiated as a debug-aid invariant. No rule change proposed.

**Ship metrics:** 2 files, +105/-2 (1 line guard expansion in VaultPageContent + 102 lines new regression test). Tests 527/527; build clean. Preview MCP skipped per capability honesty (`/plants` auth-blocked; no screenshots per chat brief). Push: `a1d371b..c45d6c6` to main per explicit yes-build greenlight.

### 2026-05-28 (IA Ship A: Plants tab promotion + FAB consistency — `9142aad` + `34e8948`)

**Plan-of-record + audit deltas:**

- **Pathname-aware delegation locked over full VaultLibraryWing extraction.** IA discussion §5.2 estimated ~3h for the Wing extraction; reading actual code revealed Library "grid" state is deeply interlocked with VaultPageContent (shared search query, gridFilters/listFilters peers, batch select per mode, refine modals). Wing extraction re-surfaces when not under feature pressure.

Matches existing nav-icon family (HomeIcon, LeafIcon, VaultIcon, CalendarIcon, JournalIcon — all inline 24×24 stroke-currentColor SVGs per VISION §8 chrome icon convention). Pass 3 sibling-sweep: nav icons are a sibling family, not FAB-tier; new addition matches the family.

Renaming to `/plants/[id]` would break 30+ deep-link sites (Calendar Plantable, Home, Garden, household-view, journal entry links, achievement badges, profile-from-grow back-button) AND break Syd + sister's existing bookmarks. Archive is a reversible state change (data preserved, can be un-archived later), not destructive. Prior red treatment (`bg-red-600`) carried false "danger" semantic and excluded Walter persona (impaired-vision-friendly emerald CTA pattern is canonical app-wide). Replaces with canonical CTA token; Cancel button also aligned to canonical FAB-form submit saga token (`border-teal-gus/40 text-teal-gus`).

**Q2 — Reverse transition (Archived → Growing un-archive UI): A (recommended) — defer to follow-up chat.** Pass 1 bidirectional state-transition trace flagged the gap (no UI surface writes `status='growing'` to an existing archived row). Phase A scope guard was "manual Archive transition" forward-only; un-archive UI deferred cleanly to next chat per scope discipline. Future chat ships an un-archive button in `vault/history/page.tsx` per-row.

**Q3 — Perennial migration mapping: A (recommended) — branched.** `harvested + is_permanent_planting=true → growing` (preserves perennial fidelity — Aria's houseplants, Maya's berries stay Growing); `harvested + annual/null → archived`; `dead → archived`. Uniform-map alternative (simpler but loses perennial nuance) rejected. Idempotent SQL — re-running maps no-ops after first application.

**Q4 — VISION §11 HarvestModal parked entry post-ship update: yes.** 2-state enum supersedes the auto-end-after-harvest model (`status: 'harvested'` is no longer a valid value). Revised recommendation: defer parked entry indefinitely; Phase A's manual-Archive model handles annual end-state realization via user action, not via auto-checkbox at harvest time. Revisit only if dogfood reveals systematic forgetting-to-Archive.

### 2026-05-28 (`inventory-polish-bundle-5items` chat — 6 inventory polish items + VISION §8 discovery-vs-lookup sort framework lock — `a51fbd7`)

**Chat purpose.** Bundle 5 polish items surfaced from Syd's 2026-05-27 dogfood of `fb5d9a0` gallery card standardization. Amendment mid-Phase-1: Syd articulated discovery-vs-lookup sort framework + extended Item 2 to include Shed → bundle becomes 6 items + 1 doc lock.

**Three asks locked at greenlight (Q1+Q2+Q3 = A on all three):**

**Q1 — Library list-view shape: Replace condensed with list (recommended).** Library binary toggle becomes gallery ↔ list. Drop `"condensed"` mode entirely; persisted-condensed users auto-migrate to gallery on next load via sessionStorage. Why: post-`c851b3d`/`fb5d9a0`, condensed is an orphan — neither a true gallery card nor a true list row. Killing it gives Library the same 2-state pattern as the 4 peer surfaces (Packets / Shed / Active Garden / My Plants). Cohesion-by-aggregation win across all 5 inventory surfaces.

**Q2 — Packets OOS-bottom trigger condition: Whenever sort = alphabetical, regardless of asc/desc (recommended).** OOS-bottom kicks in any time `sortBy === "variety"`. Why: simpler state (no "default-vs-explicit" tracking needed), semantically defensible (alphabetical reads as "show actionable items first," direction doesn't change actionability), and the `desc` case is rare enough that the simpler rule wins.

**Q3 — Sequencing: Ship all 6 at once (recommended after asks answered).** Single bounded bundle as originally scoped. Cleaner close-out than splitting into pre-ask / post-ask sub-ships.

**Framework lock — VISION §8 "Default sort by use case (discovery vs lookup)" (new sub-rule, locked 2026-05-28).** Names what was implicit per-surface and turns it into a per-category rule. Discovery surfaces (Library, Active Garden, My Plants) = most-recent first; lookup surfaces (Packets, Shed) = alphabetical by name; lookup + OOS-equivalent → OOS-bottom regardless of direction. Pairs with CLAUDE.md quick-lookup callout (same shape as other 2026-05-27 convention locks). **Library + My Plants discovery-default gap noted as parked-for-future-polish** — both currently default to alphabetical (predating the framework); framework is the source-of-truth even when current state hasn't caught up. New inventory surfaces in future ships classify first (discovery vs lookup), apply the matching default, don't re-ask per-surface.

### 2026-05-28 (earlier — Grow-now Phase 2 ship `dcfdbe4` — `grow-now-phase-2-zone-enrichment` chat)

- **Phase 2 zone-aware enrichment ✅ SHIPPED — capability gap behind feb2e32 stopgap closed.** Phase 1 (feb2e32, 2026-05-27) added honest-framing copy on Schedule + Calendar surfaces acknowledging the Zone 10b hardcoded data; Phase 2 closes the actual capability by reading `user_settings.planting_zone` server-side in `/api/seed/enrich-from-name` and instructing the Gemini research prompt to bias `planting_window` to that zone. Lazy backfill — only new profiles get zone-aware windows; existing profiles unchanged. Closes BUGS.md Post-Launch #1 capability portion. Phase 3 (multi-zone cross-profile aggregate-schedule view) stays parked.

- **Decision — server-side zone-read is authoritative.** Client-side `useUserPlantingZone()` value passed via options is for observability only (3 logEvent breadcrumbs). Why: prevents client/server zone-mismatch when user changes zone mid-flow; `fill-blanks-for-profile` transparently benefits via its internal server-to-server fetch of `enrich-from-name` (no separate wiring needed); backfill scripts keep their non-user context (passes `undefined`).

- **Decision — library-cache skipped when zone is non-10b.** `global_plant_library` has no zone column (verified via Read of route.ts:64-99 + line 142-162 upsert payload). For non-10b users we therefore skip the cache and let AI regenerate. Cost: ~1 Gemini call per never-seen-variety enrichment, bounded by same cost path that already exists for cache-miss. 10b users + unset-zone users keep library-first behavior (cost regression = zero). Future optimization: zone-keyed library cache (parked; not on any current chunk).

- **Decision — AI prompt instructs Jan-Dec month-abbreviation format regardless of zone.** Downstream `plantingWindow.ts:getDefaultSowMonthsForZone10b` parser is month-name-based (despite the "Zone10b" name, the parser is generic). New `zoneClause` template explicitly tells the AI to keep Jan/Feb/Mar/.../Dec abbreviations so the parser still flags the right months for any zone. Example outputs: zone 5a tomato "Indoor sow Feb-Mar, transplant after last frost May-Jun"; zone 9b tomato "Direct sow Mar-Apr, or Aug-Sep for fall crop"; zone 10b tomato "Spring: Feb-May" (matches existing canonical format).

- **4-pass plan-audit terminated clean iter 1.** Pass 1 factual including bidirectional state-transition matrix SKIP-with-reason (stateless background fetch — no modal/menu lifecycle, no axes to trace) + verification that `extract/route.ts:171` re-exports `researchVariety` from `@/lib/researchVariety` (so the surgical edit covers all production callers). Pass 2 concerns hunt across 9 categories incl. persona walk all 5 pass + cohesion-by-aggregation anchors named for every micro-decision (logEvent format ↔ existing scope pattern; response field shape ↔ existing snake/camel mix; prompt phrasing as explicitly-named new pattern). Pass 3 sibling sweep across 3 researchVariety callers (extract URL extraction + 2 backfill scripts pass `undefined` for backward compat) + vocab-breadth grep `zone|window|usda|hardiness|climate|sow|planting` (no missed pattern). Pass 4 lock hygiene clean — VISION §10 don't-touch untouched (no UI surface changed); §11 Phase 3 multi-zone Schedule rebuild explicitly deferred (this ship is Phase 2 only); ROADMAP §6 feb2e32 entry already named Phase 2 as the next ship (alignment confirmed).

- **Observability shape.** 3 new `logEvent("enrich", ...)` breadcrumbs in `enrichProfileFromName`: `zone_requested {profileId, userZone}` (caller fired with zone present); `zone_window_generated {profileId, userZone, window}` (API returned non-empty planting_window); `zone_fallback {profileId, reason: "no_user_zone" | "ai_no_zone_data"}` (zone unset OR AI returned empty). Server-side `console.log("[enrich-from-name] zone=X librarySkipped=Y ai=true")` confirms the route-side decision. Visible via `/settings/developer/debug-log` → Copy all → paste.

- **Test scaffolding.** New `makeSupabaseWithZone(zone)` per-table mock factory in `enrich-from-name/route.test.ts` routes `from(table)` to a table-specific chain — solves the previous "single chain for ANY table" limitation. 6 new tests cover: zone passed to researchVariety; undefined when unset; library skipped when non-10b; library kept when 10b; response includes zoneUsed; "Zone 5a" prefix normalization. `AddPlantModal.test.tsx` mocks `useUserPlantingZone` to keep existing 3 tests deterministic.

Backfill scripts — admin context (no user zone); `extract/route.ts:441` vendor URL scraping — zone-agnostic by nature. Cost optimization (zone-keyed `global_plant_library`) — future, accepted as cost-bounded for now. Schema changes — none, reuses existing `planting_window text` column.

### 2026-05-27 (small follow-up after `4c92e68` cohesion polish bundle — VISION §8 emerald-token split sub-rule + VISION §11 JournalView closure note + 4-site CTA flip)

- **Closes the two Q-asks surfaced as plain-English-at-close from `4c92e68` chat.** Both Syd-locked direction (A) per Dispatch handoff: Q1 = keep emerald-500 for state/selection + emerald-600 for CTA (document the split as a §8 sub-rule); Q2 = skip JournalView format migration + document divergence in VISION §11 as intentional closure note. Single follow-up ship bundles the doc adds with the 4-site CTA flip that the new sub-rule implies.

- **VISION §8 — new "Emerald primary-emphasis token split" subsection.** Sibling to casing / empty-state / icon-style / info-note / chevron framing / chrome control framing — same 2026-05-27 doc-architecture pattern (rule + criterion + sites + why + persona walk + GT-only). Two branches: `bg-emerald-500 text-white` = STATE / SELECTION (tab nav active, selection pill, "you are here" indicator, batch-selection checkbox, toggle-switch checked); `bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-700 text-white` = CTA / SUBMIT (Save button, primary form submit, "do this action" CTA, "Go to X" navigation trigger, primary call-to-action in empty-state card). Decision criterion: *user expected to TAP for an ACTION → emerald-600; element communicating STATE → emerald-500.* Why the split: 1-step shade difference is barely perceptible side-by-side but carries semantic meaning when the eye scans — current-state surfaces should not read as call-to-action surfaces. Same chrome-vs-content principle as the icon-style + chrome-control-framing rules applied at the color-token layer.

- **VISION §8 — legacy "Colors / brand" stub marked superseded.** The pre-existing `bg-emerald` brand-token stub (line 236-238) was "pending user confirmation" since the early design-token phase. Codebase canonical settled on `bg-emerald-600` (Tailwind direct) via the FAB-form submit saga (locked 2026-05-26 across `fc1463d` → `ba9319f`) — the brand-token aspiration remained academic. Appended one-line supersession pointer to the new sub-rule per CLAUDE.md authority-precedence "losing doc gets updated to match the winner so the conflict doesn't re-surface." Substance of the stub preserved for historical context.

- **VISION §11 — JournalView intentional-divergence closure note appended to "Cross-view consistency" entry.** Per Syd Q2 lock: JournalView ([src/app/journal/page.tsx](src/app/journal/page.tsx)) stays in its own format register (action-log shape — grouped by entry/date/plant across 3 view modes: table mobile-card / timeline plant-gallery / grid Instagram-feed) by design. Different mental model from the collection-list surfaces (Library / Packets / Shed / Active Garden / My Plants are all inventory views; Journal is an event-history view). Already shares design tokens with the unified list pattern (`rounded-xl border bg-white p-4 shadow-card card-interactive` on mobile-card mode at [journal/page.tsx:685+](src/app/journal/page.tsx:685)) so visual cohesion is preserved at the token level; shape divergence is intentional. Decision: keep distinct; don't force-fit into the condensed-list wrapper. **Cross-view-consistency parked decision (raised 2026-05-07) doesn't close — Journal is now explicitly out-of-scope; remaining cross-view work still concerns the 5 inventory surfaces only.**

### 2026-05-27 (earlier — `cohesion-polish-bundle-5items` chat — list-title font-size + Schedule child-view header + photo-card cohesion — `4c92e68`)

- **4-item cohesion polish bundle ships in one commit; 2 items surfaced as plain-English asks.** All 4 shipped items were ADJACENT findings from recent ships (`75e73d1` Packets title size, `fc338c2` photo-card A1/A2, `feb2e32` grow-now Phase 1 child-view header drift). Bundling rationale: each fix XS-size, all cohesion-only, none user-blocking; per WORKFLOW §"Batching small fixes" (3-5 items per deploy).

- **Item 1 — list-title font-size cohesion.** PacketVaultView:786 + SeedVaultView:1504 mobile-compact list titles missed explicit `text-sm` and were inheriting `text-base` (16px); ShedView:423, MyPlantsView:873, ActiveGardenView:1228 all already use explicit `text-sm` (14px). Prompt named PacketVaultView as the only outlier; Pass 3 sibling sweep caught SeedVaultView Library list as same-shape ADJACENT — included in fix. All 5 inventory list-title spans now share `text-sm` cohesion.

- **Item 2 — Schedule child-view headers drop "Zone 10b reference:" prefix.** Parent Schedule page header (`feb2e32` grow-now Phase 1) now renders zone-aware advisory conditionally; the static "Zone 10b reference:" prefix in [ActionNowView:30](src/components/schedule/ActionNowView.tsx:30) + [MonthlyPulseView:37](src/components/schedule/MonthlyPulseView.tsx:37) + [AnnualRoadmapView:54](src/components/schedule/AnnualRoadmapView.tsx:54) was redundant + risked contradicting parent's per-user advisory for non-10b zones. Dropped both the prefix AND the redundant "Reference only — not your vault." / "Reference only." trailings — parent already states "Not your vault." Children now carry just the substantive view-specific tip ("What to start or plant in {monthName}." / "Tap a month to see what the guide recommends." / "When to start indoors (blue) vs direct/outdoor (green). Vertical line = today."). Sentence case preserved per VISION §8 body-copy rule. Directly closes the `feb2e32` close-out entry's ADJACENT finding ("3 child view headers could either also become zone-aware OR drop the 'Zone 10b reference:' prefix entirely").

- **Item 4 — SeedVaultView photo-card shadow + interactive parity.** Photo-card paths ([SeedVaultView.tsx:1231](src/components/SeedVaultView.tsx:1231) + [1251](src/components/SeedVaultView.tsx:1251)) used `shadow-sm` and lacked `card-interactive`; condensed paths (1313 + 1326) use `shadow-card card-interactive`. Pass 3 sibling sweep confirmed condensed pattern is codebase consensus (ActiveGardenView:1025, Journal page:687+862+915 — all use `shadow-card card-interactive`). Photo-card was the lone outlier. Brought to baseline. `card-interactive` utility ([globals.css:62](src/app/globals.css:62)) = transition-[box-shadow,transform] 150ms + hover box-shadow + active scale(0.99) with `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` guard — additive interaction, non-breaking, no state surface touched. Directly closes the `fc338c2` close-out's ADJACENT A1/A2 findings.

### 2026-05-27 (newest — chrome control framing sub-conventions lock — doc-only)

- **VISION §8 new subsection "Chrome control framing — sub-conventions" locked.** Captures the framed-vs-unframed split for chrome controls that surfaced organically from two 2026-05-27 ships: `b339f56` (Calendar month-nav arrows dropped square frame → bare chevron-icon-only — established the UNFRAMED chevron principle) and `fc338c2` (Packets list↔grid toggle added with framed pill `rounded-xl border border-black/10 bg-white` — established the FRAMED toggle principle alongside the existing Library tab toggle). Two distinct sub-conventions named with explicit decision criterion: chrome controls representing STATE wear a frame; chrome controls representing ACTION read unframed.

- **Relationship to existing §8 subsections.** Sub-rule WITHIN the chrome lane of the chrome-vs-content icon-style split (locked earlier 2026-05-27 in `gt-icon-style-convention` chat — `cea6c71`). Icon-style sets the visual treatment of the icon (flat monotone for chrome); this convention sets the framing of the control around that icon. Orthogonal axes — both apply to chrome icons in chevron and toggle controls. Independent of §11 "App-wide icon density" parked stroke-weight decision (framing ≠ stroke weight; both can lock independently).

- **Exception captured:** photo-overlay nav (Vault profile prev/next, Shed product prev/next) keeps framed chevrons (`rounded-full bg-white/90 border w-6 h-6`) where chrome aids legibility over a photo. Honored as documented carve-out, not a contradiction of the unframed-chevron rule.

- **Quick-lookup pointer added to CLAUDE.md** as sibling to the existing Casing / Empty-cell / Icon style convention quick-lookup sections — same shape so future-Claude scans them as a coherent §8 design-token quick-reference set.

- **Persona walk:** all 5 personas pass (Maya — stateful-vs-action distinction reads as expected; Sydney — cohesion expectation met; Walter — universal-iOS convention for both shapes; Aria + Sam — less visual noise on unframed prev/next; only stateful toggles announce with a frame).

### 2026-05-27 (newest — `gt-icon-style-convention` chat — chrome vs content icon-style split lock)

- **Icon style convention locked — chrome vs content split.** Industry-standard split adopted (Apple HIG SF Symbols + Material Design icon families parallel). Locked to [VISION.md §8](docs/VISION.md) as new "Icon style — chrome vs content split" subsection — same authority-precedence shape as today's earlier casing-policy + empty-cell convention locks (visual / typographic locked design decisions belong in VISION.md per CLAUDE.md authority precedence 2026-05-16).

- **The rule (two branches):**
  - **Chrome icons** — UI structure that recurs constantly (FAB chips, nav bars, settings gears, tab icons, form-field icons, list-row affordances, modal close-X, header utility) use a **flat, monochromatic line style**. Single stroke weight, single color via `currentColor`, no fill, no illustration detail. Calm + clear + non-competing.
  - **Content icons** — emphasis on specific things the user is actively engaging with (achievement badges, plant-category markers, milestone markers, journal milestones, seasonal markers, celebratory moments, illustrated empty-state hero art) can be **illustrated, colored, or emoji-style**. These are moments, not chrome.

- **Decision criterion at audit time (one question):** *Is this icon UI structure (recurring + persistent + supports finding/tapping) or content (specific + attention-worthy)?* Chrome → flat monotone. Content → illustrated OK.

- **Worked example — FAB Add plant icon (queued semantic-fix swap).** Current FAB "Add plant" icon visually reads as a seed rather than a plant. Per this convention: icon is **chrome** (FAB primary chip, persistent + recurring + UI structure), so fix stays **flat monotone** — just needs a better-shaped plant icon from the existing Lucide library, NOT a switch to illustrated / colored / emoji-style. Same shape as 2026-05-12 chunk 3.9 #4 (Garden card "Add journal entry" trigger icon swap, `3de1c2c`) — flat icon swap within chrome lane to fix semantic mismatch, style unchanged.

- **Relationship to §11 "App-wide icon density" parked entry (preserved, NOT closed).** §11 (raised 2026-05-08 / widened 2026-05-11) asks which canonical stroke weight + size the **chrome** lane should standardize on (stroke 1.2 from `styleDictionary.tsx` vs stroke 2.0 from `navItems.tsx`). This convention sits **above** that question: §11 settles unification within the chrome lane; this convention sets the chrome-vs-content category split itself. Both are needed, neither closes the other. When §11 unlocks, its outcome applies to chrome icons defined here; content icons remain unaffected (illustrated artwork doesn't have a stroke weight).

- **Rationale.** Industry-standard split (Apple HIG SF Symbols system, Material Design icon families). Mixing styles intentionally **by role** is correct; mixing styles randomly within a single role is drift. Chrome that competes for attention exhausts the user across a long session; content that stays as flat chrome misses the emotional beat the moment is supposed to land.

- **Persona walk.** All 5 personas pass. Maya (power user) reads chrome staying calm — doesn't compete with content she scans. Sydney (cohesion) sees industry-standard split as the polished-app feel she expects. Walter (iPad-primary) reads flat monotone chrome as the SF Symbols convention; illustrated content icons read as moments worth lingering on. Aria (urban houseplant, low-data) sees chrome stay calm — never overwhelmed by FAB / nav. Sam (beginner Day 1) experiences chrome that doesn't shout, so content moments (first sprout, first harvest) actually land emotionally when they appear.

- **NORTH_STAR cite:** "Take mental load OFF the user" (chrome that stays quiet = lower cognitive load across sessions) + "No duplicate paths" (consistent chrome style IS the cohesion expression across sibling UI surfaces). Same shape as today's earlier casing-policy + empty-cell convention locks: industry-standard alignment + persona-walk validation + GT-only scope + authority-precedence remediation.

- **GT-only.** Voyager has its own visual register (parchment + in-world illustrated artwork); this convention does NOT apply there.

- **Authority-precedence remediation.** Lock destination is VISION.md §8 (canonical) + CLAUDE.md callout (quick-lookup) + ROADMAP §6 (dated log). Three-tier parallel to casing-policy + empty-cell convention locks earlier today. Per CLAUDE.md authority precedence 2026-05-16, voice / tone and locked design decisions belong in VISION.md.

- **Doc-only push tier per CLAUDE.md** — 3 files edited (VISION.md / CLAUDE.md / ROADMAP.md) + this §6 entry + §1 lead-line refresh per 2-paragraph cap; no code touched; pushed immediately after self-audit. Concurrent-fetch validation: pre-amendment `git fetch origin main` showed 0 ahead / 0 behind cleanly (Phase 2 readiness-gate item 9 ran clean).

### 2026-05-27 (later — `gt-empty-cell-convention` chat — em-dash empty-cell lock + app-wide sweep)

- **Empty-cell display convention locked — em dash "—" for empty data cells.** Industry-standard typography adopted (Apple Numbers / Google Sheets / iOS Settings / financial dashboards parallel). Locked to [VISION.md §8](docs/VISION.md) as new "Empty-cell display convention" subsection — same authority-precedence shape as the casing-policy lock 2026-05-27 (visual / typographic locked design decisions belong in VISION.md per CLAUDE.md authority precedence 2026-05-16).

- **The rule (two branches):**
  - **Use "—" for:** unambiguous "no data" cells in profile / table / detail views — Vault profile About fields (Germination / Days to Maturity / Spacing / Light / Water / Soil type when no value), plant cards' optional metadata fields, any data row where the field is structurally present but has no current value AND where there's no semantic distinction between missing / didn't-enter / doesn't-apply.
  - **Preserve semantic strings for:** fields where the displayed value carries meaning. `"None"` = user deliberately chose none. `"N/A"` = column doesn't apply to this row by design (e.g., germination time on an established-plant lifecycle path). `"Unknown"` = we tried to infer but couldn't determine (known-unknown distinct from never-entered).

- **Decision criterion at audit time (one question):** *Does this field's absence carry meaning the user needs to read?* No → "—". Yes → preserve.

- **NOT for:** loading states (use spinners / skeletons) · disabled states (use opacity / muted color) · form placeholder text (input prompts) · empty-state body copy (full-sentence 3-part frame per §3.12 #5 ship `9bad88f`).

- **Character lock:** em dash "—" = U+2014. NOT en dash "–" (U+2013), NOT hyphen-minus "-" (U+002D), NOT double-hyphen "--". Use the Unicode literal in source.

- **Phase A doc commit:** `29f37a1` — VISION.md §8 new "Empty-cell display convention" subsection + CLAUDE.md "Empty-cell convention" callout (after Casing convention) + ROADMAP §6 entry + §1 lead-line refresh per §7 2-paragraph cap.

- **Phase C sweep commit:** `0bc4342` — 20 line-edits across 7 files. **settings/developer/page.tsx** (1 — archived-planting Ended date fallback); **settings/vendors/page.tsx** (3 — formatAvg null return + group rating span + per-packet rating span); **vault/[id]/VaultProfilePacketsTab.tsx** (1 — vendor_name); **vault/[id]/page.tsx** (9 — yieldLabel + 6 About care fields: Sowing Method / Planting Window / Spacing / Sowing Depth / Sun / Water / Germination + Days to Maturity ternary); **vault/history/page.tsx** (3 — location / plantings summary / harvest_count); **components/PacketVaultView.tsx** (2 — vendor_name + purchase_date); **components/StarRating.tsx** (1 — readonly null fallback, propagates to 7 consumer files). 4-pass plan-audit terminated clean on iteration 1.

- **Preserved (no change):** all 28 "Unknown" sentinel occurrences in AI extraction routes / filter chains / matching helpers (semantic state, e.g., `plant_name !== "Unknown"` filter); 2 `<option value="">None</option>` user-choice selectors in CareScheduleManager + NewTaskModal; en-dash range separators in plantDefaults.ts (U+2013, different convention); sentence em-dashes in toasts + paragraphs; existing "—" usage at scraper-audit (5 sites) + ActiveGardenView:372 (the canonical anchor pattern). ADJACENT bucket parked for future polish: QuickAddSeed.tsx 4 sites + shopping-list/page.tsx 1 site use `|| "Unknown"` in sentence-fragment rendering — em-dash doesn't fit; different convention shape; logged for future polish pass with better empty-vendor / empty-item-name copy.

- **Rationale.** Industry-standard typography for missing data in tables and structured data displays. Single character avoids the visual weight of "--" (reads as strikethrough / dashes-as-separator) and the verbal weight of "N/A" / "None" / "Unknown" (which all imply more meaning than the absence actually carries). Apple Numbers / Google Sheets / iOS Settings convention.

- **Persona walk:** all 5 personas pass. Maya (power user) reads "—" as standard table convention; Sydney sees cohesion across profile views; Walter (iPad-primary) reads "—" as universally-recognized "no value" without learning per-app vocabulary; Aria + Sam (low-data new-user states) see less visual noise than "--" / "N/A" / "None" — empty fields visually recede instead of competing for attention.

- **NORTH_STAR cite:** "No duplicate paths" (consistent symbol IS the cohesion expression across sibling empty fields) + "Take mental load OFF the user" (single universally-recognized symbol vs per-field word). Same shape as the casing-policy lock earlier today: industry-standard alignment + persona-walk validation + GT-only scope.

- **GT-only.** Voyager has its own voice; this convention does NOT apply there unless surfaced separately.

- **Authority-precedence remediation.** Lock destination is VISION.md §8 (canonical) + CLAUDE.md callout (quick-lookup) + ROADMAP §6 (dated log). Three-tier parallel to casing-policy lock 2026-05-27. Per CLAUDE.md authority precedence 2026-05-16, voice/tone and locked design decisions belong in VISION.md.

### 2026-05-27 (latest — `gt-title-case-split` chat — casing-policy reversal + app-wide sweep)

- **Casing policy split locked — Title Case for headers + buttons, sentence case for body.** Industry-standard split adopted (Apple HIG / Material Design / iOS Settings parallel). Locked to [VISION.md §8](docs/VISION.md) as new "Casing (headers + buttons vs body)" subsection — promotes the rule from previously-only-ROADMAP-dated entries into a durable design token, closing the doc-architecture gap flagged via authority-precedence audit (locked design decisions belong in VISION.md per CLAUDE.md authority precedence 2026-05-16; the prior casing rule was logged only in dated ROADMAP §6 entries).

- **AP-style Title Case mechanic locked.** Articles (`a`, `an`, `the`) + short conjunctions (`and`, `but`, `or`, `nor`, `for`, `yet`, `so`) + prepositions ≤4 letters (`in`, `on`, `to`, `of`, `by`, `at`, `for`, `with`, `from`, `into`, `onto`, `over`, `up`) lowercase mid-string. First + last word ALWAYS capitalized regardless of part of speech. Prepositions 5+ letters capitalize (`Through`, `Without`, `After`, `Across`). Compound-verb particles capitalize (`Sign Up`, `Log Out`). Examples: `Save to Vault` · `Add to Shed` · `When to Plant (by Zone)` · `Continue to Import Review` · `Overwrite with AI?` · `Save for Later` · `At a Glance`. **Counter-recommendation considered + rejected:** every-word Title Case — simpler mental model but less iOS-conventional + reads marketing-shouty on longer labels.

- **Reverses** the implicit "all sentence case" cohesion bar that operated 2026-05-24 → 2026-05-27 — specifically reverts 2026-05-24 `006dd69` Item 2 sentence-cased form headers + Q4 widen of option labels in choose-steps + 2026-05-25 `a78dbd6` 22-edit FAB-tree sweep (HEADERS + BUTTONS lanes only; field labels / aria-labels / enum tokens / longer body copy / QUICK_ACTIONS / supply categories / volume pills stay sentence case per the body lane preservation in VISION.md §8 taxonomy).

- **Phase A doc commit:** `3ee1063` — VISION.md §8 new "Casing" subsection + CLAUDE.md "Casing convention" callout + lineage updates on 2026-05-24 + 2026-05-25 ROADMAP entries.

- **Phase C sweep commit:** `5b5617c` — 59 files / +133/-132. Full inventory in `.claude/plans/gt_title_case_split.md` §4.1-§4.2. Headers: page h1 + modal h2 + section h2 + tracking-uppercase sub-headers sites. Buttons: form submit + secondary CTA + chip / option labels in choosers. Tab labels (`Plant Profiles` / `Seed Vault`). Settings menu row labels. Test assertions updated where touched (AddPlantModal.test.tsx + calendarBatchSelect.regression.test.ts — prevents cc5e65b-shape e2e drift). 438/438 tests passing; clean build.

- **Preserved (no change):** field labels above inputs (Plant name / Variety / cultivar / Vendor / nursery) · aria-labels matching field labels · volume pills (Full / Partial / Low / Empty as enum tokens) · QUICK_ACTIONS labels (Pot up / Plant out / Cold stratify — enum tokens) · supply category tokens (Fertilizer / Pesticide / Other) · helper text / placeholders · toast messages · Journal day-rotating prompts · empty-state bodies · page-label proper nouns (`Active Garden`, `My Plants`, `Plant Profiles`, `Seed Vault`, `Plant This Month`).

- **NORTH_STAR cite:** "No duplicate paths" (consistent casing IS the cohesion expression across sibling labels) + industry-standard alignment (Apple HIG / Material Design / iOS Settings split). Persona walk: all 5 personas pass (Maya scans labels → Title Case meets expectations; Walter iPad-primary → standard iOS app feel; Sydney → cohesive; Aria + Sam empty-state Title-Case-title-vs-sentence-case-body = clear info hierarchy).

- **Authority-precedence remediation logged.** Previous casing locks lived only in dated ROADMAP §6 entries, never in VISION.md. Per CLAUDE.md authority precedence locked 2026-05-16, voice/tone and locked design decisions belong in VISION.md. Today's amendment closes the gap.

### 2026-05-27 — CLAUDE.md Pass 1 audit rule add (post-FAB-tree polish bundle dogfood)

- **Bidirectional state-transition tracing locked as Pass 1 subcategory in CLAUDE.md.** Three consecutive drift instances in the 2026-05-26 FAB-tree polish bundle (`7c0decf` items 1+2 + `84df090` item 8 + `c124213` item 9) all had the same root shape: asymmetric tracing across an axis of state transition. **Item 1+2:** code analysis traced the OPEN path correctly but missed the BACK path (same axis, different direction); bug persisted for weeks, caught only by Syd's dogfooding. **Item 8:** chunk-fetch latency hypothesis preloaded modal chunks on FAB-menu open, missed the Suspense first-render gap (different React axis — lazy resolution, not chunk fetch); fix shipped, didn't close the reported bug. **Item 9:** finally caught the Suspense + lazy-resolution gap via pre-resolving React.lazy through unconditional mount; took 3 hypothesis revisions to land. New rule: for any modal/menu lifecycle change, Pass 1's factual trace must cover state transitions in BOTH directions (open/close/forward/back) AND across React commit-phase axes (reconciliation, Suspense + lazy resolution, mount lifecycle). Matrix approach forces every relevant axis onto the plan pre-commit. **When a fix doesn't close the reported bug, the next hypothesis MUST move to a different cell of the matrix — refining the same axis is the drift shape this catches.** ~60-90s cost per affected change; far cheaper than one wasted ship cycle (item 8 → item 9 alone cost 2 ship cycles + Vercel deploys). Pairs complementary with existing Pass 2 cohesion-by-aggregation (catches new-pattern introduction) and persona-walk (catches user-exclusion concerns); Pass 1 subcategory catches **factual tracing completeness** on the state-transition surface.

- **Doc-only push tier per CLAUDE.md** — single-file CLAUDE.md amendment + this §6 changelog entry; no code touched; pushed immediately after self-audit. Concurrent-fetch validation #14: pre-amendment `git fetch origin main` showed 0 ahead / 0 behind cleanly. Phase 2 readiness-gate item 9 (canonical-doc divergence check before amendment) ran clean.

### 2026-05-18

- **§3.12 catalog theme #5 ✅ SHIPPED (`9bad88f`, `trusting-proskuriakova-8e23c2` chat, 2026-05-18).** Empty-state cliff audit + per-surface copy rewrite across the app's 6 EmptyStateCard sites + 14 raw-card / inline `<p>` empty states. **17 code files / ~22 distinct copy strings touched** (~30 edit operations counting collapsed `isNewUser` variants). Resolves §3.12 catalog theme #5 — Sam day-1 risk (cliff-style "No X yet" framing replaced with invitation framing across every surface user lands on day 1) + Walter low-tech-comfort (jargon dropped across body copy: "permanent," "perennial" body, "polyculture," "FAB," "Vault import," "active batches," "Map your hillside," "Plant from the Seed Vault").

  **Per-surface 3-part frame** anchored as the cohesion primitive: purpose-describing title / plain next-step body / verb-led CTA. Every empty state in the app now reads as an invitation, not a cliff.

  **Key autonomous design decisions (per dispatch contract — routine copy phrasing is autonomous; surfaced via Phase 1 plan-relay before greenlight):**
  1. **3-part frame anchor (title / body / verb-led CTA)** — chosen as the cohesion anchor across all 22 distinct copy strings. Picked over alternatives like 2-part (title + body only) or sentence-frame because verb-led CTA standardization is what bottoms out paradox-of-choice for Sam day-1.
  2. **CTA standardization "Add a {noun}"** — chosen over "Add your first {noun}" (excludes mature-state returning users) and "Add {noun}" (less personal/inviting). Walter-tested: works for both first-time + returning. Sam-tested: singular, not paradoxical.
  3. **"Long-living plants"** chosen over "permanent plants" / "perennial plants" as the Walter-plain replacement. "Permanent" reads botanically-wrong (plants die); "perennial" is correct jargon but Walter friction. "Long-living" describes the user-observable property in plain words.
  4. **"Library" softens "Vault"/"Shed" in body copy only** — page-level labels preserved (theme #3 Phase A territory). "Your seed library starts here" reads warmer than "Your Vault is empty." Body-vs-label split is intentional cohesion guard: theme #3 will rename the page labels separately + holistically.
  5. **`isNewUser` branch collapse in V1/V2/S1/G1** — new copy reads correctly for both first-time + returning users, so the per-branch ternary becomes dead complexity. Small code-complexity reduction; behavior preserved; Pass 1 verified `isNewUser` had no other consumers.
  6. **J1 day-rotating prompts preserved unchanged** — the prompt array at [journal/page.tsx:639-650](src/app/journal/page.tsx:639) is already on-voice; replacing it would be over-reach. Only the empty-state title and CTA hint copy changed; the rotating prompts kept intact.

  **Boundaries respected (Pass 4 lock-hygiene):**
  - **VISION §10 empty-by-default LOCK preserved verbatim.** This ship refines COPY ON existing empty states; it does NOT add notifications, tasks, or state-by-default. OnboardingDock untouched. The Sam day-1 fix is copy-only — the principle that empty IS the onboarding stays locked.
  - **§3.12 theme #2 (outdoor-garden assumption sweep)** — light touch only. "Fruit trees, bushes" → "trees, bushes, or anything else you keep year after year" generalizes outdoor framing; full outdoor sweep (page-level renames "Active Garden," "Plantable," beds-as-default) remains theme #2 work.
  - **§3.12 theme #3 (plain-language audit)** — body-level only. Walter jargon dropped in body copy across all surfaces; page-label renames ("Vault," "Shed," "Plantable") remain theme #3 Phase A. Body-vs-label split prevents pre-empting theme #3's holistic rename map.
  - **§3.12 theme #7 (cross-view consistency)** — primitive-canonicalization on raw-card empty states captured as ADJACENT and parked to §4. 4 surfaces use `bg-white rounded-xl border ... p-8 text-center` raw-card shape instead of canonical `EmptyStateCard` primitive. Revised to `LANGUAGE plpgsql STABLE` with `RAISE EXCEPTION 'Not authorized' USING ERRCODE = '42501'`. - **§3.12-tester T3 ✅ LOCKED (Option A — public stays as-is). Doc-only ship (`flamboyant-lamport-f5cc74` chat, 2026-05-17).** Three options surfaced (A public / B existing tap-unlock / C new tester allowlist); user picked Recommended Option A via Rule A. ZERO code change — feedback button stays public on all 3 sites ([AuthGuard.tsx:195](src/components/AuthGuard.tsx:195) loading-shell mobile top bar + [AuthGuard.tsx:297](src/components/AuthGuard.tsx:297) post-auth mobile top bar + [Sidebar.tsx:162](src/components/Sidebar.tsx:162) desktop sidebar footer). Pre-sign-in auth page already shows zero feedback buttons (all 3 sites wrapped in `{!isAuthPage}`).

  **Decision rationale:** app-store distribution locked 2026-05-17 (VISION §1, §3) inverts the calculus pre-app-store. Pre-app-store, "tester-only feedback" made sense — user + sister were the only testers. Post-app-store-locked, public users are exactly who we want feedback from on launch; gating cuts off that channel. Feedback button ≠ developer tool — §3.12-pre's `4a8b04c` resolved destructive admin actions visible to fresh users (fill-in-blanks, extract cache, import logs); feedback is the opposite: user-to-developer communication, common public-app pattern. Apps that hide feedback behind hidden gestures look like they're avoiding accountability — bad signal at launch.

  **Process lesson captured to memory:** Pass 3 sibling-sweep grep regex must cover **vocabulary breadth**, not just the obvious naming for the pattern you expect. When gating dev tools, search for `DeveloperUnlock`, `tapVersion`, `isUnlocked` alongside env-var patterns. The cost of a too-narrow regex = parallel-mechanism failure mode (the specific cohesion-by-aggregation drift CLAUDE.md 2026-05-14 locked against). Caught here pre-commit by luck (the stale test mock had the existing context's name in it); next time the regex should catch it deliberately.

- **Sharing-purpose chat closed end-to-end (`competent-blackwell-5de2a2`, 2026-05-17). All 6 open-territory items (a)-(f) from VISION §11 resolved + 4 bonus locks (public boundary, sharing data model, persona system, app-store distribution context) shipped in same chat.** Non-build design chat per Chat Lifecycle Protocol; Phases 2-4 no-ops; Phase 1 (state purpose + surface conflicts + propose resolutions) + Phase 5 (capture decisions into VISION + new PERSONAS.md + CLAUDE.md) carried the load. **10 decisions locked:**

  1. **Public boundary** → 🕐 long-term in VISION §9. "Never public" stays as *current* boundary; not a forever-lock. Revisit post-MVP if user pull emerges. Reason: differentiator is private accumulated knowledge per VISION §2; opening public pulls into category (Greg, Planta, PictureThis) where leaders exist and moat collapses; infrastructure cost (moderation, abuse, content review) ≈ second app inside this one. User signal verbatim: *"maybe thats a long term pin? ... idk if its better to build the public side? or keep it internal with invite only 'communities'."* User-direction-contradicts-locked-rule path followed: surfaced explicitly, surfaced trade-off, recommendation locked direction.

  2. **Sharing data model = communication + transfer-at-time.** NO pre-marked "shareable" state on plants or items. Removes entire lifecycle-state-management complexity (greenhouse vs garden split, marked-then-planted contradiction, quantity-share-marking). Sharing happens via communication (browse → request → approve, OR board post → claim) + transfer at approval time. User surfaced the underlying complexity (sister's 180-seed-start scenario; *"what if she marks them as shareable, but then starts planting?"*) which forced the simplification.

  3. **Privacy controls = per-category opt-in** (not per-item). Default: nothing shared with circle. User opts in by CATEGORY (seed packets / active plants / harvests / etc.) per group. Manageable even at power-user scale (180+ items).

  4. **Trusted-circle internal structure = groups with mode.** Each group has: members, mode (browse OR board), name. Default "Friends & Family" browse-mode group auto-created on first circle member added. Members can be in multiple groups (e.g. sister in "Family" browse + "Vista Gardeners" board). User signal verbatim: *"should we have different layers to your members? like when you add someone, you can choose whether its open free for all lol or if its community the request board?"* Resolved as per-group-mode (not per-member-mode) so board surface coheres as a group-shared feed.

  5. **Club request-board flows (A/B/C) locked.** Flow A: Post an ASK → others respond/claim. Flow B: Post an OFFER → others claim. Flow C: Browse the board feed. Per-post opt-in (nothing exposed by default). Coordination on multi-responder claims TBD at build time.

  6. **Trade lifecycle = two shapes, both auto-log to Journal.** Shape 1 (direct give): long-press plant/packet → "Give / trade" → pick recipient from browse-mode group members → confirm → Journal entry. Shape 2 (broadcast offer): from board-mode group surface → "Post an offer" → someone claims → kicks off Shape 1 → Journal entry. No dedicated Trades tab. Button conditional-renders (hidden when user has no circle). Persona-walk confirmed: works for Maya / Sydney / Walter / Aria / Sam; solo users + Sam never see the button (no clutter).

  7. **Notifications differentiated by interaction type, not relationship layer.** Direct interactions (incoming request, approval, trade complete) → push by default. Ambient activity (board posts, others' general updates) → pull-only. Household coordination ("BF watered tomatoes 2hr ago") → opt-in light push (off by default). NO activity feed at any layer. New VISION §10 don't-touch entry locks "no activity feed."

  8. **Household attribution = auto-record + default-hide + filter-on-demand.** Data layer captures who did each action (already happens via `user_id`). Default UI shows no person ("watered 2hr ago"). One opt-in filter view ("show actions by [person]") surfaces attribution when wanted. Minimal MVP UX cost: one filter UI surface (likely on Journal or per-plant action history).

  9. **Persona system locked as new process tool.** 5 personas: Maya (Power Gardener) / Sydney (Spring-Planner Hobbyist) / Walter (Retiree Gardener) / Aria (Houseplant Urban User) / Sam (First-Time Beginner). Captured in new `docs/PERSONAS.md`. Referenced from CLAUDE.md plan-audit standard as Pass 2 + Pass 3 "persona walk" subcategory. User signal verbatim: *"would it be a good idea to mock up different users and use them as a 'thought review' as we go through our build?"* User was already applying the persona lens in real-time (pushed back on first trade-home recommendation as *"way too specific and is not applicable to every user if i put this app on the store"*). Formalizing makes the check consistent.

  10. **App-store / public-distribution context made explicit.** Updates VISION §1 boundaries (new line) + §3 first paragraph (now explicit "intended for public release / app-store distribution") + this ROADMAP §6 entry + CLAUDE.md "What this project is" section (refined from "single user has been testing personally" to "user is product owner; intended for public release"). User signal verbatim: *"do we need to note in our roadmap that im building this app for public use/selling/app store?"* Foundational context that should have been explicit from day one — was implicit ("home gardeners across the full skill range") but never named. Implication: every UX decision must generalize beyond user's specific scenario. Reinforces the persona-walk discipline.

- **Migration audit ran against prod Supabase via column-dump diagnostic.** Schema_migrations tracking table doesn't exist (user has been applying migrations manually via Dashboard SQL Editor, not via `supabase db push` CLI). Fallback: `SELECT table_name, column_name, data_type FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_schema='public'` chunked in 3 alphabetical buckets due to Dashboard's 100-row UI cap. Cross-referenced against all ~100 migrations in `supabase/migrations/`. **Result:** only ONE additional column gap found beyond the U24 one — `user_settings.onboarding_completed_at`. All other column-additive migrations are applied. `journal_entries.entry_type` CHECK constraint verified current (11 values including `cold_stratify` from 2026-03-19 migration `20260319120000_journal_entry_type_cold_stratify.sql` — which means even 2026-dated migrations are reaching prod). **Out of audit scope:** RLS policies, RPC functions, triggers, indexes, storage policies. ~10 migrations affect those — could have separate gaps. Not investigated this turn.

- **Migration-naming process bug locked: duplicate timestamp prefix `20250330000000` caused silent migration skip.** Two migration files share the exact same timestamp prefix: `20250330000000_journal_entry_type_prune.sql` and `20250330000000_user_settings_onboarding_complete.sql`. Supabase migration ordering uses the prefix — when prefixes collide, ordering is undefined and one can be silently skipped by `supabase db push` or by Dashboard application order. Prune was applied to prod; onboarding_completed_at wasn't. **Same root cause likely produced the original U24 `ended_at` gap** (need to investigate timestamps around `20250207500000` / `20250207600000` for similar collisions — not done this turn). **Process fix proposed for future migrations:** use unique `YYYYMMDDHHMMSS` timestamps (14 digits with actual hour/minute/second) instead of `YYYYMMDD000000` (8 digits + 6 zeros). Captured to ROADMAP §3.10 as a new R-item.

- **U25 captured to BUGS — My Plants cross-surface icon mismatch with Active Garden.** Discovered during phone-verify of `3de1c2c` (chunk 3.9 #4 garden trigger icon swap): Active Garden gallery + list use `<ICON_MAP.Edit />` (pen-with-motion); My Plants list uses inline SVG of a notebook at [MyPlantsView.tsx:893](src/components/MyPlantsView.tsx:893). Same action ("Add journal entry") reads with two different icons. Strict bug per VISION §4 principle 3. Root cause: `3de1c2c` scoped to ActiveGardenView only — MyPlantsView wasn't named in scope. The cohesion-by-aggregation rule (locked 2026-05-14) would have caught this in Pass 2 had it existed at the time of the ship. Validates the rule's named failure mode in retrospect. Fix scoped: 2-line code change + 1 import + regression test extension + Preview MCP. Deferred to follow-up chat.
